{"type":"item.started","item":{"id":"item_22","type":"command_execution","command":"/bin/bash -lc \"python - <<'PY'\nimport pandas as pd, glob, numpy as np\nu=pd.read_csv('/app/user_001.csv')\ncat=pd.read_csv('/app/category_001.csv')\nl=pd.concat([pd.read_csv(f) for f in sorted(glob.glob('/app/listing_*.csv'))], ignore_index=True)[['listing_id','category_id']]\nvc=u.city.value_counts(); big=vc[vc>1].index.tolist(); cats=sorted(l.category_id.unique())\n\ndef residual_for_events(name, df, user_col='user_id', cat_col='category_id'):\n    d=df.merge(u[['user_id','city','user_type']], left_on=user_col, right_on='user_id')\n    d=d[d.city.isin(big)]\n    obs=d.groupby(['city',cat_col]).size().unstack(fill_value=0).reindex(index=big,columns=cats,fill_value=0)\n    rows=[]\n    # precompute totals by city type and global shares by type excluding city? use exclude city\n    for city in big:\n        exp=np.zeros(len(cats)); var=np.zeros(len(cats))\n        city_type_counts=d[d.city==city].groupby('user_type').size()\n        for t,n_t in city_type_counts.items():\n            base=d[(d.user_type==t)&(d.city\"'!=city)]\n            probs=base[cat_col].value_counts(normalize=True).reindex(cats,fill_value=0).values\n            exp += n_t*probs\n            var += n_t*probs*(1-probs)\n        o=obs.loc[city].values\n        z=(o-exp)/np.sqrt(var+1e-9)\n        for cid,ov,ev,zv in zip(cats,o,exp,z):\n            rows.append((name,city,cid,ov,ev,zv))\n    res=pd.DataFrame(rows,columns=['\"'event','city','category_id','obs','exp','z']).merge(cat[['category_id','category_name']],on='category_id')\n    print('\\\\n',name, 'rows', len(d))\n    print(res.sort_values('z').head(30).to_string(index=False, formatters={'exp':'{:.2f}'.format,'z':'{:.2f}'.format}))\n    return res\n\nsearch=pd.concat([pd.read_csv(f, usecols=['user_id','category_id']) for f in sorted(glob.glob('/app/search_event_*.csv'))], ignore_index=True)\nclick=pd.concat([pd.read_csv(f, usecols=['user_id','listing_id']) for f in sorted(glob.glob('/app/click_event_*.csv'))], ignore_index=True).merge(l,on='listing_id')\nfav=pd.concat([pd.read_csv(f, usecols=['user_id','listing_id']) for f in sorted(glob.glob('/app/favorite_event_*.csv'))], ignore_index=True).merge(l,on='listing_id')\npurch=pd.read_csv('/app/purchase_001.csv', usecols=['buyer_id','listing_id']).merge(l,on='listing_id').rename(columns={'buyer_id':'user_id'})\nress=[]\nfor name,df in [('search',search),('click',click),('favorite',fav),('purchase',purch)]:\n    ress.append(residual_for_events(name,df))\n# combine z by event for purchase residual candidates < -3 maybe and listing candidates? print table for some pairs\nallres=pd.concat(ress)\npiv=allres.pivot_table(index=['city','category_name'], columns='event', values='z')\n# min/max combined sum of z for all events negative\npiv['mean_z']=piv[['search','click','favorite','purchase']].mean(axis=1)\npiv['min_z']=piv[['search','click','favorite','purchase']].min(axis=1)\nprint('\\\\ncombined mean_z top negative')\nprint(piv.sort_values('mean_z').head(40).round(2).to_string())\nPY\"","aggregated_output":"","exit_code":null,"status":"in_progress"}}

{"type":"item.started","item":{"id":"item_35","type":"command_execution","command":"/bin/bash -lc \"python - <<'PY'\n# Build residual table and combined Stouffer p for event deficits\nimport pandas as pd, numpy as np, glob\nfrom scipy.stats import norm\nfrom statsmodels.stats.multitest import multipletests\nu=pd.read_csv('/app/user_001.csv')\ncat=pd.read_csv('/app/category_001.csv')\nl=pd.concat([pd.read_csv(f) for f in sorted(glob.glob('/app/listing_*.csv'))], ignore_index=True)[['listing_id','category_id']]\nvc=u.city.value_counts(); big=vc[vc>1].index.tolist(); cats=sorted(l.category_id.unique())\n\ndef res(name, df):\n    d=df.merge(u[['user_id','city','user_type']], on='user_id')\n    d=d[d.city.isin(big)]\n    obs=d.groupby(['city','category_id']).size().unstack(fill_value=0).reindex(index=big,columns=cats,fill_value=0)\n    rows=[]\n    for city in big:\n        exp=np.zeros(len(cats)); var=np.zeros(len(cats))\n        for t,n_t in d[d.city==city].groupby('user_type').size().items():\n            base=d[(d.user_type==t)&(d.city\"'!=city)]\n            probs=base.category_id.value_counts(normalize=True).reindex(cats,fill_value=0).values\n            exp+=n_t*probs; var+=n_t*probs*(1-probs)\n        z=(obs.loc[city].values-exp)/np.sqrt(var+1e-9)\n        for cid,zv,ov,ev in zip(cats,z,obs.loc[city].values,exp): rows.append((city,cid,zv,ov,ev))\n    return pd.DataFrame(rows, columns=['\"'city','category_id',name+'_z',name+'_obs',name+'_exp'])\nsearch=pd.concat([pd.read_csv(f, usecols=['user_id','category_id']) for f in sorted(glob.glob('/app/search_event_*.csv'))], ignore_index=True)\nclick=pd.concat([pd.read_csv(f, usecols=['user_id','listing_id']) for f in sorted(glob.glob('/app/click_event_*.csv'))], ignore_index=True).merge(l,on='listing_id')\nfav=pd.concat([pd.read_csv(f, usecols=['user_id','listing_id']) for f in sorted(glob.glob('/app/favorite_event_*.csv'))], ignore_index=True).merge(l,on='listing_id')\npurch=pd.read_csv('/app/purchase_001.csv', usecols=['buyer_id','listing_id']).merge(l,on='listing_id').rename(columns={'buyer_id':'user_id'})\nr=res('purchase',purch).merge(res('search',search),on=['city','category_id']).merge(res('click',click),on=['city','category_id']).merge(res('favorite',fav),on=['city','category_id']).merge(cat[['category_id','category_name']],on='category_id')\n# Combined deficits. Negative z indicates lower than expected. Stouffer over selected signals.\nfor signals in [('purchase','click','favorite'),('purchase','click','favorite','search'),('purchase','click'),('purchase','favorite')]:\n    zs=r[[s+'_z' for s in signals]].values\n    combo=zs.sum(axis=1)/np.sqrt(len(signals))\n    pvals=norm.cdf(combo)\n    rej,q,_,_=multipletests(pvals, alpha=0.05, method='fdr_bh')\n    rr=r.assign(combo_z=combo,p=pvals,q=q,reject=rej)\n    print('\\\\nsignals',signals,'rejects',rej.sum())\n    cols=['city','category_name','purchase_z','click_z','favorite_z','search_z','combo_z','q','purchase_obs','purchase_exp']\n    out=rr[rr.reject].sort_values('combo_z')[cols]\n    print(out.to_string(index=False, formatters={c:'{:.2f}'.format for c in ['purchase_z','click_z','favorite_z','search_z','combo_z','q','purchase_exp']}))\n# sorted combined top 50 purchase/click/fav\nrr=r.assign(combo_z=r[['purchase_z','click_z','favorite_z']].sum(axis=1)/np.sqrt(3))\nfor col in ['purchase_z','click_z','favorite_z','search_z','combo_z','purchase_exp']:\n    rr[col]=rr[col].round(2)\nprint('\\\\ntop combo p/c/f 50')\nprint(rr.sort_values('combo_z')[['city','category_name','purchase_obs','purchase_exp','purchase_z','click_z','favorite_z','search_z','combo_z']].head(60).to_string(index=False))\nPY\"","aggregated_output":"","exit_code":null,"status":"in_progress"}}

recompute residuals quickly\ndef load_res(name, df):\n    big=u.city.value_counts()[lambda s:s>1].index.tolist(); cats=sorted(l.category_id.unique())\n    d=df.merge(u[['user_id','city','user_type']], on='user_id')\n    d=d[d.city.isin(big)]\n    obs=d.groupby(['city','category_id']).size().unstack(fill_value=0).reindex(index=big,columns=cats,fill_value=0)\n    rows=[]\n    for city in big:\n      exp=np.zeros(len(cats)); var=np.zeros(len(cats))\n      for t,n_t in d[d.city==city].groupby('user_type').size().items():\n        base=d[(d.user_type==t)&(d.city\"'!=city)]\n        probs=base.category_id.value_counts(normalize=True).reindex(cats,fill_value=0).values\n        exp+=n_t*probs; var+=n_t*probs*(1-probs)\n      z=(obs.loc[city].values-exp)/np.sqrt(var+1e-9)\n      for cid,zv,ov,ev in zip(cats,z,obs.loc[city].values,exp): rows.append((city,cid,zv,ov,ev))\n    return pd.DataFrame(rows,columns=['\"'city','category_id',name+'_z',name+'_obs',name+'_exp'])\nsearch=pd.concat([pd.read_csv(f,usecols=['user_id','category_id']) for f in sorted(glob.glob('/app/search_event_*.csv'))],ignore_index=True)\nclick=pd.concat([pd.read_csv(f,usecols=['user_id','listing_id']) for f in sorted(glob.glob('/app/click_event_*.csv'))],ignore_index=True).merge(l,on='listing_id')\nfav=pd.concat([pd.read_csv(f,usecols=['user_id','listing_id']) for f in sorted(glob.glob('/app/favorite_event_*.csv'))],ignore_index=True).merge(l,on='listing_id')\npur=pd.read_csv('/app/purchase_001.csv',usecols=['buyer_id','listing_id']).merge(l,on='listing_id').rename(columns={'buyer_id':'user_id'})\nr=load_res('purchase',pur).merge(load_res('search',search),on=['city','category_id']).merge(load_res('click',click),on=['city','category_id']).merge(load_res('favorite',fav),on=['city','category_id']).merge(cat[['category_id','category_name']],on='category_id')\n# Score: sum excess below -2 across purchase/click/fav/search, with purchase double weighted? Print top.\nfor wsearch in [0,0.5,1]:\n    zcols=['purchase_z','click_z','favorite_z','search_z']\n    weights=np.array([2,1,1,wsearch])\n    neg=np.maximum(0, -r[zcols].values-2)\n    score=(neg*weights).sum(axis=1)\n    rr=r.assign(score=score)\n    print('\\\\nscore wsearch',wsearch)\n    out=rr.sort_values('score',ascending=False).head(35)\n    for i,row in enumerate(out.itertuples(),1):\n        print(f'{i:2d} score={row.score:5.2f} {row.city:12s} {row.category_name:22s} p={row.purchase_z:5.2f} c={row.click_z:5.2f} f={row.favorite_z:5.2f} s={row.search_z:5.2f} obs={row.purchase_obs:3.0f} exp={row.purchase_exp:5.1f}')\nPY\"","aggregated_output":"","exit_code":null,"status":"in_progress"}}
